       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Two lost souls hook up for a night of alcohol fueled passion but a year later, they have to work together as a team. Jack wasn’t the only one keeping his home life very private. AU
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Jack gestured for her to go into the kitchen and as he followed, he couldn’t help but let his gaze wander. He had never seen the captain out of her BDUs or combat gear and he decided that she had a nice figure. He knew that already though, as a flashback of their first meeting entered his mind, but seeing her dressed in civvies, in his home, seemed to reinforce the thought tenfold.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

            <textarea cols="50" id="embed_code_481612168" rows="4">&lt;a href="https://archiveofourown.org/works/17534309"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;What's Your Poison?&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt; (2260 words) by &lt;a href="https://archiveofourown.org/users/wackyjacqs"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;wackyjacqs&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Chapters: 1/1&lt;br /&gt;Fandom: &lt;a href="https://archiveofourown.org/tags/Stargate%20SG-1"&gt;Stargate SG-1&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Rating: General Audiences&lt;br /&gt;Warnings: No Archive Warnings Apply&lt;br /&gt;Relationships: Samantha "Sam" Carter/Jack O'Neill&lt;br /&gt;Characters: Samantha "Sam" Carter, Jack O'Neill&lt;br /&gt;Additional Tags: Team Bonding&lt;br /&gt;Series: Part 24 of &lt;a href="https://archiveofourown.org/series/1234973"&gt;Bizarre Holidays&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Summary: &lt;p&gt;Jack gestured for her to go into the kitchen and as he followed, he couldn’t help but let his gaze wander. He had never seen the captain out of her BDUs or combat gear and he decided that she had a nice figure. He knew that already though, as a flashback of their first meeting entered his mind, but seeing her dressed in civvies, in his home, seemed to reinforce the thought tenfold.&lt;/p&gt;</textarea>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         “Carter,” a little puff of air ruffles her fringe as he sighs, “please tell me you’re – that sweater – that you’ve – ”
        </p>
        <p>
         He refuses to meet Sam’s gaze, but given their close proximity, he feels every movement as she slowly shakes her head.
        </p>
        <p>
         “No, sir.”
        </p>
        <p>
         “Yeah,” he murmurs, “that’s what I figured.”
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         In the weeks after the events at the Alpha Site, Sam can't sleep and Hammond sends her home. Pete calls, determined to help her through. But one thing is absolutely crystal clear: she knows for a fact that if she decides she needs someone tonight, it will not be Pete that she calls.
        </p>
        <p>
         Which is exactly why Colonel Jack O'Neill is in her kitchen right now.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         "Hi. Um. God, I feel silly doing this. But it’s only an old laptop, I guess. Not too much to lose apart from my dignity.. Okay. Phew. So here goes. Hello SG-1! If that’s what you’re called in your version of the universe. If that mirror that looked like the quantum mirror from that episode of SG-1 is actually a quantum mirror... I’m willing to take the chance."
        </p>
        <p>
         It's 2019, and the SGC awakens to a laptop from earth - an alternate earth where Stargate was a TV show like Wormhole Xtreme. A laptop filled with fanfiction from a site called AO3 and an interview with Amanda Tapping and Richard Dean Anderson, where they discuss Sam and Jack's feelings for each other.
        </p>
        <p>
         --oOo--
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         “For… my commanding officer?” Heat flushed across my cheeks before I could chase it away.
        </p>
        <p>
         Alyssa’s wizened face crinkled into her smile. “What a quaint term! You T’auri are still remarkably patriarchal for such an advanced civilisation”
        </p>
        <p>
         My blush turned crimson as I understood her meaning. “No! No, not in that sense!” I stammered. “He’s in charge of me. At work. We just work together!”
        </p>
       </blockquote>

         As ridiculous as it may seem, she doesn’t know how to process the information, because even though they’ve virtually lived in each other’s pockets for six years now – this is the first time she remembers seeing him without his shoes and socks.
        </p>
       </blockquote>
